The campus looked dazzling with a splash of tricolor almost on all the quarters of the school. Students of Class VII presented a thematic assembly and set the spirits of the patriotism high. The enactment presented by the students was on Unity in Diversity and showed the integrity we could project as a Nation. The school choir, dressed in their Tricolor attires, presented numbers dedicated to the motherland. The kindergartners also contributed to the assembly with their group song \u201cNanha Munna Rahi Hoon\u201d.  ',  Principal of the school Mr.S.N.Shukla addressed the students and asked them to play their role as a student to contribute to the positive growth of the nation.', +5', Delhi Public School Patiala',  added ', 2 new photos', .',   ', 8 March 2016',   ', The Woman Power at Delhi Public School Patiala was evident when the educators met to share their thoughts on the prevailing issues of women. Shukla  commended the teachers for their untiring efforts in churning out the potential of the students and in being able to do justice in the various roles that life offered them.', Delhi Public School Patiala',  added a new photo.',   ', 24 February 2016',   ', Delhi Public School Patiala',  added a new photo.',   ', 31 December 2015',   ', Delhi Public School Patiala',  added ', 23 new photos', .',   ', 15 December 2015',   ', Delhi Public School Patiala had its 3rd Annual Winter Carnival \u201cChristmas Mania\u201d in its sprawling campus. The mega event was inaugurated by Mr.Rajesh Tripathi, ADC (Development) . The event drew huge crowds not only from the city of Patiala, but also from  the neighboring suburbs of Sirhind and Nabha. Children and adults, alike, could be seen thronging in the various game stalls. The multi-cuisine stalls offering tingling and tasty winter snacks attracted the crowds in huge n', ...', umbers. The Christmas spirit was lifted higher with the Christmas Carols wafting through. Children were thrilled with all the rides though the Buggy Ride with Santa was a run-away hit. The highlight of the event was the Baby Show \u201cGiggles & Coos\u201d.  ',  The fun-filled event came to a close with the announcing of the Lucky Draw.',  The Pro Vice Chairman of the School, Mr.Ramesh Talwar and Principal Mr.S.N.Shukla congratulated the DPS Team in organizing the mega event and making it a huge success. They also conveyed their festive wishes for Christmas and the coming New Year to all those who made it to the event.',  ', See more', +20', Delhi Public School Patiala',  added a new photo.',   ', 9 December 2015',   ', Delhi Public School Patiala',  added ', 21 new photos', .',   ', 3 November 2015',   ', A few bits of making of Annual Function...', +18', Delhi Public School Patiala',   ', 28 October 2015',   ', Dear Readers ',  We need to clearly state that this ',  facebook page belongs to Delhi  Public School Patiala,which functions under the aegis of Delhi Public School Society, New Delhi. Thanks.', Delhi Public School Patiala',  added ', 16 new photos', .',   ', 27 September 2015',   ', The Kindergarten Section celebrated The Gandparent's Day. The school was decorated to taste to welcome the special guests- the grandpas and the grandmas. They came in good numbers out of love for their grandchildren who were highly thrilled to see them in the school. A lot of games and activities were planned for the occasion and each aspect was enjoyed by the guests... be it the awareness quiz, memory game, "paar ki nazar" , "geet gata chal" ; it was the pure happiness to watch the spirit of the grandparents as they completed with each other. The dance floor was populated with the grandparents tapping their feet to the hits from yesteryear. The occasion came to an end with refreshments and tea.', +13', See more', Delhi Public School, Patiala was established in 2013 under the aegis of Delhi Public School Society. The campus looked dazzling with a splash of tricolor almost on all the quarters of the school. Students of Class VII presented a thematic assembly and set the spirits of the patriotism high. The enactment presented by the students was on Unity in Diversity and showed the integrity we could project as a Nation. The school choir, dressed in their Tricolor attires, presented numbers dedicated to the motherland. The kindergartners also contributed to the assembly with their group song \u201cNanha Munna Rahi Hoon\u201d.  ',  Principal of the school Mr.S.N.Shukla addressed the students and asked them to play their role as a student to contribute to the positive growth of the nation.', +5', Delhi Public School Patiala',  added ', 2 new photos', .',   ', 8 March 2016',   ', The Woman Power at Delhi Public School Patiala was evident when the educators met to share their thoughts on the prevailing issues of women. The mega event was inaugurated by Mr.Rajesh Tripathi, ADC (Development) . The event drew huge crowds not only from the city of Patiala, but also from  the neighboring suburbs of Sirhind and Nabha. Children and adults, alike, could be seen thronging in the various game stalls. The multi-cuisine stalls offering tingling and tasty winter snacks attracted the crowds in huge n', ...', umbers. The Christmas spirit was lifted higher with the Christmas Carols wafting through. Children were thrilled with all the rides though the Buggy Ride with Santa was a run-away hit. The highlight of the event was the Baby Show \u201cGiggles & Coos\u201d.  ',  The fun-filled event came to a close with the announcing of the Lucky Draw.',  The Pro Vice Chairman of the School, Mr.Ramesh Talwar and Principal Mr.S.N.Shukla congratulated the DPS Team in organizing the mega event and making it a huge success. The school was decorated to taste to welcome the special guests- the grandpas and the grandmas. They came in good numbers out of love for their grandchildren who were highly thrilled to see them in the school. A lot of games and activities were planned for the occasion and each aspect was enjoyed by the guests... be it the awareness quiz, memory game, "paar ki nazar" , "geet gata chal" ; it was the pure happiness to watch the spirit of the grandparents as they completed with each other. The dance floor was populated with the grandparents tapping their feet to the hits from yesteryear.
